This list contains users from `Venezuela` and cities `Caracas` `Maracay` `Maracaibo` `Guayana-city` `Barquisimeto` `Maturin` `Cumana` `Petare` `Turmero` `Bolivar-city` `Barinas` `Los-teques` `Punto-fijo` `La-guaira` `Santa-teresa-del-tuy` `El-vigia` `San-felipe-del-rey` `Puerto-la-cruz` `Cabimas` `Guatire` `Porlamar` `Guarenas` `San-fernando-de-apure` `Los-guayos` `Upata` `Ocumare-del-tuy` `Puerto-cabello` `Guacara` `Machiques` `Naguanagua` `Acarigua` `Coro` `Valera` `Cabudare` `Charallave` `Ciudad-ojeda` `Tariba` `San-juan-de-los-morros` `La-villa-del-rosario` `Yaritagua` `Mariara` `Guanare` `Carupano` `Araure` `Ejido` `Carora` `Guasdualito` `La-grita` `Guama` `Rubio` `Bocon√≥` `Nirgua` `Sa-antonio-de-los-altos` `San-jose-de-guanipa` `Tinaquillo` `Guigue` `Chivacoa` `Caripito` `San-antonio-del-tachira` `Cantaura` `Puerto-ayacucho` `Ospino` `Lecheria` `Pampatar` `Guanta` `Higuerote` `Colonia-tovar` `Tucacas` `Puerto-piritu`.

There are `16 countries` and `191 cities` can be found [here](https://github.com/hbourgeot/top-github-users).

There are `993 users`  in Venezuela. You need at least `6 followers` to be on this list.

## üì¶ Third party

- [@octokit/graphql](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@octokit/graphql) - Send GraphQL requests to GitHub API.
- [fs-extra](https://www.npmjs.com/package/fs-extra) - Creating directories and files.
- [simple-git](https://www.npmjs.com/package/simple-git) - Handling Git commands.
